<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">oele</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">owl</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, <span class="ann-pos">a dialectal form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uil.html>uil</a></i></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wapper.html>wapper</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:oelewapper.html>oelewapper</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a large moth; a simpleton; fool</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***oen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oen.html>oen</a> (8481)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Uncertain, probably Germanic, possibly related to loen, okkeloen or oekeloen and/or to the Frisian given name Oene
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oen.html>oen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oenen.html>oenen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oen.html>oentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A nincompoop, moron, dumb person</li>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:uur.html>Uur</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ōra</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ūra-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ferriferous sand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)wūr-</i>.  However, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Irish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Irish language">Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ga">úir</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">soil, earth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*auraz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a> earth, sand, mud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oer.html>oer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>ferrous ground, sand clotted by iron(III) oxide, bog iron ore</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">ijzeroer</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:oer.html>oer</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">oer-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mens.html>mens</a></i>, likely a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Urmensch</i>.

</p>
<ol><li>A prehistoric human, especially an apeman. <span class="defdate">[from late 1860s]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A primitive human, considered uncivilised. <span class="defdate">[from late 19th c.]</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oever.html>oever</a> (10028)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:oever.html>oever</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*uovar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ōferaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oever.html>oever</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oevers.html>oevers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oever.html>oevertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bank (as in riverbank), shore (e.g. of a lake)
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2005</b>,  “<span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>Aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oevers.html>oevers</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a></span>”, in  <cite><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:Dagen_van_gras,_dagen_van_stro" class="extiw" title="w:nl:Dagen van gras, dagen van stro"><a href = vnd.unilang:dagen.html>Dagen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gras.html>gras</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dagen.html>dagen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stro.html>stro</a></a></span></cite>, performed by <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:Spinvis" class="extiw" title="w:nl:Spinvis">Spinvis</a></span>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oeverloos.html>oeverloos</a> (102276)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oever.html>oever</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">riverbank</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-loos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-less, without</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>shoreless</li>
<li>continuing on and on without any progress or result; boundless
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> word <a href = vnd.unilang:moe.html>moe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:oeverloos.html>oeverloze</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:discussies.html>discussies</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:politiek.html>politiek</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I'm getting tired of all the discussions <b>without result</b> in politics.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ofer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ofer.html>ofer</a> (102274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*uber</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*upér</i>, a comparative form of <i>*upo</i>.
</p><p><i>Germanic cognates:</i> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">oƀar</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">ubar</i> (whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">über</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">yfir</i> (whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">över</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌿𐍆𐌰𐍂</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ufar</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p><i>Indo-European cognates:</i> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὑπέρ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hupér</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:super.html>super</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Irish">Old Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga">for</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">gor-</i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latinx headword" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:ofer.html>ofer</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>, above</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latinx headword" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:ofer.html>ofer</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+dative, of a location</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>, above, beyond</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+accusative, of motion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>, across</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ōferaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

***officier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:officier.html>officier</a> (1764)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:officier.html>officier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">official</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:officier.html>officier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">officiārius</i>.
</p><p>The sense “overseer” <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">overseer</i>.
</p>

***oink.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oink.html>oink</a> (74001)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Imitative of the sound.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:oink.html>oink</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>Representing the sound made by a pig.</li>
<li>Drawing attention to male chauvinism (from the term <i>male <a href = vnd.unilang:chauvinist.html>chauvinist</a> pig</i>).
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1982</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:sandy.html>Sandy</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:asher.html>Asher</a>,  <cite>Just like Jenny‎</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Mom swallowed a spoonful of <a href = vnd.unilang:pudding.html>pudding</a> and looked Daddy straight in the eye. "<b><a href = vnd.unilang:oink.html>Oink</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:oink.html>oink</a>," she <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a>, to let him know he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> being a male <a href = vnd.unilang:chauvinist.html>chauvinist</a> pig.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>2003</b>, Robert N. Mansfield, <a href = vnd.unilang:randy.html>Randy</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maas.html>Maas</a>, <i>The Assassin: Attack on America</i>
<dl><dd>"The tub <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> too small!" "Then, I'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> go first and you'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> have to wait!" "<a href = vnd.unilang:chauvinist.html>Chauvinist</a> pig!" "<b><a href = vnd.unilang:oink.html>Oink</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:oink.html>oink</a>!"</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2005</b>,  Alinka Zyrmont,  <cite>Forbidden Passion</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">You are such a male <a href = vnd.unilang:chauvinist.html>chauvinist</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:oink.html>oink</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:oink.html>oink</a>. You think that you are the only one who can drive a car or fly an airplane.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:oink.html>oink</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">oinks</b>)
</p>

</td></tr></tbody></table>
<ol><li>The sound made by a pig, or an imitation thereof.
<dl><dd><i>The protesters replied to the police <a href = vnd.unilang:officers.html>officers</a>' demands with a chorus of <b>oinks</b>.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">grunt</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:oink.html>oink</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">oinks</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">oinking</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">oinked</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Of a pig or in imitation thereof, to make its characteristic sound.
<dl><dd><i>The hogs <b>oinked</b> happily in their <a href = vnd.unilang:pen.html>pen</a> as the farmer poured <a href = vnd.unilang:slop.html>slop</a> in their feeding trough.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***oksel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oksel.html>oksel</a> (33976)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ocsele</i>, either from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*uokusala</i> or borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">axele</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ahslō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shoulder</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*aḱs-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:armpit.html>armpit</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">axle</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:armpit.html>armpit</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Achsel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:armpit.html>armpit</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">axilla</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:armpit.html>armpit</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">axis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">axle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,
<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Greek language">Greek</a></span> <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">άξονας</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">áxonas</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">axle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">अक्ष</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ákṣa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">axle</span><span ***oliebol.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oliebol.html>oliebol</a> (59866)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:olie.html>olie</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">oil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bol.html>bol</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bun</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oliebol.html>oliebol</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oliebollen.html>oliebollen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oliebol.html>oliebolletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:oliebol.html>oliebol</a></span>, a traditional Dutch and Belgian delicacy normally consumed on New Year's Eve or at funfairs

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:olm.html>olm</a> (114809)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:olm.html>olm</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> (only attested in toponyms), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*elmaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:olm.html>olm</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:olmen.html>olmen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:olm.html>olmpje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An elm, tree of the genus <i>Ulmus</i>.</li></ol>

***om.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> (35)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ombe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">omme</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">umbi</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">umbe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*umbi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_2">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>around, about</li>
<li>at (a time)</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>convinced, persuaded
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rechter.html>rechter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The judge <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> persuaded.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">The judge <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></b>.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>up; <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a> (time)
